<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.80.83.E8.B3.87.E6.96.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參考資料">參考資料</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%AC%A1%E8%B2%B8%E5%8D%B1%E6%A9%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="编辑章节：參考資料">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li id="cite_note-148"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-148">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a href="/wiki/%E8%92%82%E8%8E%AB%E8%A5%BF%C2%B7F%C2%B7%E8%93%8B%E7%89%B9%E7%B4%8D" title="蒂莫西·F·蓋特納">蒂莫西·F·蓋特納</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.newyorkfed.org/newsevents/speeches/2008/tfg080609.html">Geithner-Speech Reducing Systemic Risk in a Dynamic Financial System</a>. 紐約聯邦儲備銀行. 2008-06-09 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2009-03-23</span>]</span>. （原始内容<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.webcitation.org/68F26RF6v?url=http://www.newyorkfed.org/newsevents/speeches/2008/tfg080609.html">存档</a>于2012-06-07）. <q>In early 2007, asset-backed commercial paper conduits, in structured investment vehicles, in auction-rate preferred securities, tender option bonds and variable rate demand notes, had a combined asset size of roughly $2.2 trillion. Assets financed overnight in triparty repo grew to $2.5 trillion. Assets held in hedge funds grew to roughly $1.8 trillion. The combined balance sheets of the then five major investment banks totaled $4 trillion. In comparison, the total assets of the top five bank holding companies in the United States at that point were just over $6 trillion, and total assets of the entire banking system were about $10 trillion." He stated that the "combined effect of these factors was a financial system vulnerable to self-reinforcing asset price and credit cycles.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%AC%A1%E8%B2%B8%E5%8D%B1%E6%A9%9F&amp;rft.au=%E8%92%82%E8%8E%AB%E8%A5%BF%C2%B7F%C2%B7%E8%93%8B%E7%89%B9%E7%B4%8D&amp;rft.btitle=Geithner-Speech+Reducing+Systemic+Risk+in+a+Dynamic+Financial+System&amp;rft.date=2008-06-09&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.pub=%E7%B4%90%E7%B4%84%E8%81%AF%E9%82%A6%E5%84%B2%E5%82%99%E9%8A%80%E8%A1%8C&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.newyorkfed.org%2Fnewsevents%2Fspeeches%2F2008%2Ftfg080609.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook" class="Z3988"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-149"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-149">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%9D%E7%BE%85%C2%B7%E5%85%8B%E9%AD%AF%E6%A0%BC%E6%9B%BC" class="mw-redirect" title="保羅·克魯格曼">保羅·克魯格曼</a>. The Return of Depression Economics and the Crisis of 2008. W.W. Norton Company Limited. 2009. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-0-393-07101-6" title="Special:网络书源/978-0-393-07101-6"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-0-393-07101-6</a>. <q>As the shadow banking system expanded to rival or even surpass conventional banking in importance, politicians and government officials should have realized that they were re-creating the kind of financial vulnerability that made the Great Depression possible--and they should have responded by extending regulations and the financial safety net to cover these new institutions. Influential figures should have proclaimed a simple rule: anything that does what a bank does, anything that has to be rescued in crises the way banks are, should be regulated like a bank.</q></cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%AC%A1%E8%B2%B8%E5%8D%B1%E6%A9%9F&amp;rft.au=%E4%BF%9D%E7%BE%85%C2%B7%E5%85%8B%E9%AD%AF%E6%A0%BC%E6%9B%BC&amp;rft.btitle=The+Return+of+Depression+Economics+and+the+Crisis+of+2008&amp;rft.date=2009&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-393-07101-6&amp;rft.pub=W.W.+Norton+Company+Limited&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook" class="Z3988"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
